        (tipe_aset = 'Hibah' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park' AND lokasi != 'Rusak') OR
        (tipe_aset = 'Titipan' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park' AND lokasi != 'Rusak') OR
        (tipe_aset = 'Peminjaman Vendor Insiden' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park' AND lokasi != 'Rusak') OR
        (tipe_aset = 'Sewa Vendor' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park' AND lokasi != 'Rusak') OR
        (tipe_aset = 'Sewa - Rental Vendor' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park' AND lokasi != 'Rusak') OR
        (tipe_aset = 'Peminjaman Vendor' AND status_aset = 'Aktif' AND lokasi_asset = 'Sudirman Park')
    ) ORDER BY 
                            CASE 
                                WHEN parent_id IS NOT NULL THEN 0 
                                ELSE 1                          
                            END,
                            parent_id,                      
                            sn_child,  
                            CASE 
                                WHEN level_parent = 'Unit' THEN 1        
                                WHEN level_parent = 'Module' THEN 2       
                                WHEN level_parent = 'Sub Module' THEN 3   
                                ELSE 4                                      
                            END;
